# ЁЯУЪ Day 2: Blog Index Page тАУ Show All Posts with Links

---

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржорж░рж╛ ржХрзА ржХрж░ржмрзЛ?

- рж╕ржм Markdown ржлрж╛ржЗрж▓ ржерзЗржХрзЗ title, date ржУ slug ржмрзЗрж░ ржХрж░ржмрзЛ  
- `/blog` ржкрзЗржЬрзЗ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржмрзЛ:  
  ЁЯФЧ Post Title (as link)  
  ЁЯУЕ Date

---

## тЬЕ рзи. Step-by-Step

---

### ЁЯУБ Step 1: Update `lib/posts.js` тАУ getSortedPosts()

```js
export function getSortedPosts() {
  const fileNames = fs.readdirSync(postsDir);

  const posts = fileNames.map(fileName => {
    const slug = fileName.replace(/\.md$/, '');
    const filePath = path.join(postsDir, fileName);
    const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
    const { data } = matter(fileContent);

    return {
      slug,
      ...data
    };
  });

  return posts.sort((a, b) => (a.date < b.date ? 1 : -1));
}
```

---

### ЁЯУБ Step 2: Create Blog Index Page

`pages/blog/index.js`

```jsx
import Link from 'next/link';
import { getSortedPosts } from '../../lib/posts';
import Head from 'next/head';

export default function BlogIndex({ posts }) {
  return (
    <>
      <Head>
        <title>All Blog Posts</title>
      </Head>
      <main style={{ padding: "20px" }}>
        <h1>ЁЯУЭ Blog Posts</h1>
        <ul>
          {posts.map(post => (
            <li key={post.slug}>
              <Link href={`/blog/${post.slug}`}>
                <strong>{post.title}</strong>
              </Link>
              <br />
              <small>{post.date}</small>
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </main>
    </>
  );
}

export async function getStaticProps() {
  const posts = getSortedPosts();
  return {
    props: { posts }
  };
}
```

---

## тЬЕ Result:

тЮбя╕П ржПржЦржи `/blog` ржкрзЗржЬрзЗ рж╕ржм Markdown ржкрзЛрж╕рзНржЯрзЗрж░  
тЬФя╕П Title (with link to `/blog/[slug]`)  
тЬФя╕П Date  
тЬФя╕П Sorted by latest first

---

## ЁЯОп Bonus: `Layout.js` ржпрзЛржЧ ржХрж░рзЗ Navbar ржмрж╕рж╛рждрзЗ ржкрж╛рж░рзЛ

```jsx
<Link href="/">Home</Link> | <Link href="/blog">Blog</Link>
```

---

## тЬЕ ржЖржЬржХрзЗрж░ рж╢рзЗржЦрж╛:

| ржмрж┐рж╖рзЯ | ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЦрзНржпрж╛ |
|------|----------|
| Blog Listing | рж╕ржм ржкрзЛрж╕рзНржЯ ржПржХрж╕рж╛ржерзЗ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржирзЛ |
| Dynamic Link | `/blog/${slug}` ржмрж╛ржирж╛ржирзЛ |
| Static Props | Build time ржП ржбрзЗржЯрж╛ ржЖржирж╛ |
| Sorting | ржирждрзБржи ржкрзЛрж╕рзНржЯ ржЖржЧрзЗ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржирзЛ |

---

## ЁЯЫая╕П ржкрзНрж░рзНржпрж╛ржХржЯрж┐рж╕:

1. ржЖрж░ржУ Markdown ржкрзЛрж╕рзНржЯ ржпрзЛржЧ ржХрж░рзЛ  
2. рж╕ржм ржкрзЛрж╕рзНржЯ `/blog` ржП ржарж┐ржХржарж╛ржХ рж▓рж┐рж╕рзНржЯ рж╣ржЪрзНржЫрзЗ ржХрж┐ржирж╛ ржжрзЗржЦрзЛ  
3. рж▓рж┐рж╕рзНржЯрзЗ date ржлрж░ржорзНржпрж╛ржЯ рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ ржХрж░рзЗ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржУ (ржпрзЗржоржи `April 2, 2025`)

## тЭУ ржХрзБржЗржЬ:

ЁЯСЙ `getStaticProps()` ржХржЦржи ржЪрж╛рж▓рж╛рзЯ?  
A. ржкрзНрж░рждрж┐ reload

### ЁЯФЬ ржЖржЧрж╛ржорзАржХрж╛рж▓ (Day 3):  
**Blog Card Design with Tailwind CSS тАУ рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ UI**  
рждрзБржорж┐ ржХрж┐ ржЪрж╛ржУ ржЖржорж┐ ржПржЦржиржЗ Tailwind ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ Blog Card ржбрж┐ржЬрж╛ржЗржи рж╢рзЗржЦрж╛ржЗ? ЁЯШДЁЯОи

# ЁЯОи Day 3: Blog Card UI with Tailwind CSS

---

## тЬЕ рзз. Tailwind CSS Setup (ржпржжрж┐ ржЖржЧрзЗ ржирж╛ ржХрж░рзЛ)

Next.js-ржП Tailwind CSS ржпрзБржХрзНржд ржХрж░рж╛рж░ ржЬржирзНржп (рззржмрж╛рж░ржЗ ржХрж░рждрзЗ рж╣рзЯ):

```bash
npm install -D tailwindcss postcss autoprefixer
npx tailwindcss init -p
```

ЁЯУД `tailwind.config.js`

```js
content: [
  "./pages/**/*.{js,ts,jsx,tsx}",
  "./components/**/*.{js,ts,jsx,tsx}"
],
```

ЁЯУД `styles/globals.css`

```css
@tailwind base;
@tailwind components;
@tailwind utilities;
```

ЁЯУД `_app.js`

```js
import '../styles/globals.css';
```

---

## тЬЕ рзи. Blog Card Design тАУ `/pages/blog/index.js`

ржЖржорж░рж╛ ржПржЦржи Tailwind ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ card-style post listing ржХрж░ржмрзЛред

---

### ЁЯУШ Updated `pages/blog/index.js`

```jsx
import Link from 'next/link';
import Head from 'next/head';
import { getSortedPosts } from '../../lib/posts';

export default function BlogIndex({ posts }) {
  return (
    <>
      <Head>
        <title>Blog | Hamid</title>
      </Head>
      <main className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 py-10">
        <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-6">ЁЯУЭ Blog Posts</h1>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
          {posts.map((post) => (
            <Link key={post.slug} href={`/blog/${post.slug}`}>
              <div className="border rounded-xl p-5 shadow hover:shadow-md transition bg-white">
                <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">{post.title}</h2>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">{post.date}</p>
                <p className="mt-2 text-gray-600">
                  Read more тЖТ
                </p>
              </div>
            </Link>
          ))}
        </div>
      </main>
    </>
  );
}

export async function getStaticProps() {
  const posts = getSortedPosts();
  return {
    props: { posts },
  };
}
```

---

## тЬЕ Output UI:

- ЁЯУж Clean white card
- ЁЯЧУя╕П Title + Date
- ЁЯЦ▒я╕П Hover ржП shadow
- ЁЯза Responsive: ржорзЛржмрж╛ржЗрж▓рзЗ 1 ржХрж▓рж╛ржо, рж▓рзНржпрж╛ржкржЯржкрзЗ 2

```js
import { format } from 'date-fns';

return {
  slug,
  ...data,
  date: format(new Date(data.date), 'MMMM dd, yyyy')
};
```

тЮбя╕П Output: `April 02, 2025`

```bash

```

# ЁЯУЦ Day 4: Blog Detail Page (Slug) тАУ Typography + SEO + Design

---

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржорж╛ржжрзЗрж░ рж▓ржХрзНрж╖рзНржп:

- рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ ржХрж░рзЗ ржЯрж╛ржЗржЯрзЗрж▓, рждрж╛рж░рж┐ржЦ, ржХржиржЯрзЗржирзНржЯ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржирзЛ  
- Meta Tag (SEO ржУ Social Share ржЬржирзНржп)  
- Typography style (markdown тЖТ HTML)  
- Readable layout with spacing

---

## тЬЕ рзи. Blog Slug Page ржЖржкржбрзЗржЯ ржХрж░рж╛

ЁЯУД `pages/blog/[slug].js`

```jsx
import Head from 'next/head';
import { getAllPostSlugs, getPostData } from '../../lib/posts';
import { remark } from 'remark';
import html from 'remark-html';

export default function BlogPost({ title, date, contentHtml }) {
  return (
    <>
      <Head>
        <title>{title} | Blog</title>
        <meta name="description" content={`Read: ${title}`} />
        <meta property="og:title" content={title} />
        <meta property="og:description" content={`Blog by Hamid`} />
      </Head>

      <main className="max-w-3xl mx-auto px-4 py-10">
        <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-2">{title}</h1>
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mb-6">{date}</p>

        <article
          className="prose prose-lg max-w-none"
          dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: contentHtml }}
        />
      </main>
    </>
  );
}

export async function getStaticPaths() {
  const paths = getAllPostSlugs();
  return { paths, fallback: false };
}

export async function getStaticProps({ params }) {
  const post = getPostData(params.slug);
  const processedContent = await remark().use(html).process(post.content);
  const contentHtml = processedContent.toString();

  return {
    props: {
      title: post.title,
      date: post.date,
      contentHtml
    }
  };
}
```

---

## тЬЕ рзй. Tailwind Typography Plugin (prose class)

ЁЯСЙ Markdown ржХржиржЯрзЗржирзНржЯ рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ ржХрж░рждрзЗ ржПржЗ plugin ржмрзНржпржмрж╣рж╛рж░ ржХрж░ржмрзЛред

```bash
npm install @tailwindcss/typography
```

ЁЯУД `tailwind.config.js`

```js
plugins: [
  require('@tailwindcss/typography'),
],
```

тЮбя╕П ржПржЦржи `prose` ржХрзНрж▓рж╛рж╕ ржХрж╛ржЬ ржХрж░ржмрзЗ тЮЬ рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ H1, p, ul, code styling

---

## тЬЕ рзк. SEO Meta Tags ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЦрзНржпрж╛:

| Tag | ржХрж╛ржЬрзЗ рж▓рж╛ржЧрзЗ |
|-----|------------|
| `<title>` | ржмрзНрж░рж╛ржЙржЬрж╛рж░рзЗ title ржУ SEO |
| `<meta name="description">` | Google snippet |
| `og:title`, `og:description` | Facebook/LinkedIn preview |
| `og:image` (Bonus) | ржерж╛ржорзНржмржирзЗржЗрж▓ рж╢рзЗрзЯрж╛рж░ ржЗржорзЗржЬ

| ржмрж┐рж╖рзЯ | ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЦрзНржпрж╛ |
|------|----------|
| Markdown тЖТ HTML | Content рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ржнрж╛ржмрзЗ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржирзЛ |

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржорж╛ржжрзЗрж░ ржЯрж╛рж░рзНржЧрзЗржЯ:

- Logged-in (or admin only) user тЖТ Add Post Button ржжрзЗржЦрждрзЗ ржкрж╛рж░ржмрзЗ  
- Public user тЖТ рж╢рзБржзрзБ ржкрзЛрж╕рзНржЯ ржкрзЬрждрзЗ ржкрж╛рж░ржмрзЗ

## тЬЕ рзи. ржзрж░рж┐ рждрзБржорж┐ ржЖржЧрзЗржЗ `next-auth` ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ рж▓ржЧржЗржи рж╕рж┐рж╕рзНржЯрзЗржо ржХрж░ржЫрзЛ  
рждрж╛рж╣рж▓рзЗ `useSession()` ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ ржЗржЙржЬрж╛рж░ access ржкрж╛ржмрзЗред

---

### ЁЯУШ `pages/blog/index.js` тАУ Add Post Button (Admin Only)

```jsx
import { useSession } from 'next-auth/react';

...

export default function BlogIndex({ posts }) {
  const { data: session } = useSession();

  return (
    <main className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 py-10">
      <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-6">ЁЯУЭ Blog Posts</h1>

      {session?.user?.email === "your@email.com" && (
        <div className="mb-4">
          <a
            href="/admin/create"
            className="inline-block bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded hover:bg-blue-700"
          >
            тЮХ New Post
          </a>
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
        {posts.map((post) => (
          <Link key={post.slug} href={`/blog/${post.slug}`}>
            <div className="border rounded-xl p-5 shadow hover:shadow-md transition bg-white">
              <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">{post.title}</h2>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">{post.date}</p>
              <p className="mt-2 text-gray-600">Read more тЖТ</p>
            </div>
          </Link>
        ))}
      </div>
    </main>
  );
}
```

## тЬЕ рзй. Admin Page рждрзИрж░рж┐ ржХрж░рзЛ (Placeholder)

ЁЯУД `pages/admin/create.js`

```jsx
import { useSession } from 'next-auth/react';

export default function CreatePost() {
  const { data: session } = useSession();

  if (session?.user?.email !== "your@email.com") {
    return <p className="text-center p-10">тЫФ Unauthorized Access</p>;
  }

  return (
    <main className="max-w-2xl mx-auto px-4 py-10">
      <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4">Create New Post</h1>
      <p>This page will later include form to add Markdown files.</p>
    </main>
  );
}
```

# ЁЯУК Week 6 тАУ Day 1: Admin Dashboard Layout with Sidebar + Topbar

---

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржЬржХрзЗрж░ рж▓ржХрзНрж╖рзНржп:

- Layout component рждрзИрж░рж┐ ржХрж░ржмрзЛ  
- Sidebar (navigation) ржПржмржВ Topbar (logo + logout) ржерж╛ржХржмрзЗ  
- рж╕ржм Dashboard page ржПрж░ ржоржзрзНржпрзЗ ржПржЗ layout reuse ржХрж░ржмрзЛ  
- Tailwind ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ UI ржмрж╛ржирж╛ржмрзЛ

---

## тЬЕ рзи. Project Structure (for dashboard):

```
pages/
тФЬтФАтФА dashboard/
тФВ   тФЬтФАтФА index.js         тЖТ Dashboard Home
тФВ   тФФтФАтФА users.js         тЖТ Users Table Page (later)
components/
тФЬтФАтФА DashboardLayout.js   тЖТ Sidebar + Topbar
тФФтФАтФА SidebarLink.js       тЖТ Sidebar menu link
```

---

## тЬЕ рзй. Step-by-Step: DashboardLayout

ЁЯУД `components/DashboardLayout.js`

```jsx
import Link from "next/link";

export default function DashboardLayout({ children }) {
  return (
    <div className="flex h-screen bg-gray-100">
      {/* Sidebar */}
      <aside className="w-64 bg-white shadow-md p-4 hidden md:block">
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">Admin Panel</h2>
        <ul className="space-y-3">
          <li><Link href="/dashboard" className="text-blue-600">ЁЯУК Dashboard</Link></li>
          <li><Link href="/dashboard/users">ЁЯСе Users</Link></li>
          <li><Link href="#">тЪЩя╕П Settings</Link></li>
        </ul>
      </aside>

      {/* Main Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col">
        {/* Topbar */}
        <header className="bg-white shadow p-4 flex justify-between items-center">
          <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold">Welcome Admin</h1>
          <button className="text-sm text-red-600">Logout</button>
        </header>

        {/* Page content */}
        <main className="p-6 overflow-y-auto">{children}</main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## тЬЕ рзл. Tailwind UI Explanation

| ржХрзНрж▓рж╛рж╕ | ржХрж╛ржЬ |
|------|-----|
| `flex` | Layout ржмрж╛ржирж╛ржирзЛ |
| `h-screen` | ржлрзБрж▓ рж╕рзНржХрзНрж░рж┐ржи рж╣рж╛ржЗржЯ |
| `bg-gray-100` | рж╣рж╛рж▓ржХрж╛ ржмрзНржпрж╛ржХржЧрзНрж░рж╛ржЙржирзНржб |
| `shadow-md` | ржмржХрзНрж╕ рж╢рзНржпрж╛ржбрзЛ |
| `p-4`, `p-6` | ржкрзНржпрж╛ржбрж┐ржВ |
| `text-xl`, `font-bold` | ржмрзЬ ржУ ржорзЛржЯрж╛ рж▓рзЗржЦрж╛ |

# ЁЯУЛ Day 2: Responsive User Table UI with Tailwind CSS

---

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржорж╛ржжрзЗрж░ рж▓ржХрзНрж╖рзНржп:

- User list ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржмрзЗ ржЯрзЗржмрж┐рж▓ ржЖржХрж╛рж░рзЗ  
- ржкрзНрж░рждрж┐ row-рждрзЗ: ржирж╛ржо, ржЗржорзЗржЗрж▓, рж░рзЛрж▓  
- Table scrollbar ржерж╛ржХржмрзЗ  
- Future ready: API ржерзЗржХрзЗ data load ржХрж░рж╛ ржпрж╛ржмрзЗ

---

## тЬЕ рзи. Dummy Data рждрзИрж░рж┐ ржХрж░рзЛ

ЁЯУД `data/users.js`

```js
const users = [
  {
    id: 1,
    name: "Hamid Uddin",
    email: "hamid@example.com",
    role: "Admin",
  },
  {
    id: 2,
    name: "Sadia Rahman",
    email: "sadia@example.com",
    role: "Editor",
  },
  {
    id: 3,
    name: "Nusrat Jahan",
    email: "nusrat@example.com",
    role: "Viewer",
  },
];

export default users;
```

---

## тЬЕ рзй. Create User Table Page

ЁЯУД `pages/dashboard/users.js`

```jsx
import DashboardLayout from "@/components/DashboardLayout";
import users from "@/data/users";

export default function UsersPage() {
  return (
    <DashboardLayout>
      <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">ЁЯСе Users</h2>

      <div className="overflow-x-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-4">
        <table className="min-w-full table-auto text-left">
          <thead>
            <tr className="bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 uppercase text-sm leading-normal">
              <th className="py-3 px-6">Name</th>
              <th className="py-3 px-6">Email</th>
              <th className="py-3 px-6">Role</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody className="text-gray-700 text-sm">
            {users.map((user) => (
              <tr key={user.id} className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">
                <td className="py-3 px-6 font-medium">{user.name}</td>
                <td className="py-3 px-6">{user.email}</td>
                <td className="py-3 px-6">
                  <span className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold
                    ${user.role === "Admin" ? "bg-red-100 text-red-600" :
                      user.role === "Editor" ? "bg-blue-100 text-blue-600" :
                        "bg-gray-100 text-gray-600"}`}>
                    {user.role}
                  </span>
                </td>
              </tr>
            ))}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </DashboardLayout>
  );
}
```

---

## тЬЕ рзк. Tailwind Explanation:

| ржХрзНрж▓рж╛рж╕ | ржХрж╛ржЬ |
|------|-----|
| `overflow-x-auto` | ржЫрзЛржЯ рж╕рзНржХрзНрж░рж┐ржирзЗ ржЯрзЗржмрж┐рж▓ scroll рж╣рзЯ  
| `table-auto` | Table layout auto adjust  
| `bg-white rounded shadow` | рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ ржХрж╛рж░рзНржбрзЗрж░ ржорждрзЛ ржЯрзЗржмрж┐рж▓  
| `hover:bg-gray-50` | рж╣рзЛржнрж╛рж░ ржЗржлрзЗржХрзНржЯ  
| `badge-style role` | Role ржЕржирзБржпрж╛рзЯрзА рж░ржЩ

---

## тЬЕ рзл. Output:

тЬФя╕П рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ ржЯрзЗржмрж┐рж▓  
тЬФя╕П ржорзЛржмрж╛ржЗрж▓-ржлрзНрж░рзЗржирзНржбрж▓рж┐  
тЬФя╕П рж╣рзЛржнрж╛рж░ ржЗржлрзЗржХрзНржЯ  
тЬФя╕П Role ржПрж░ ржнрж┐рждрзНрждрж┐рждрзЗ ржХрж╛рж▓рж╛рж░

## ЁЯза ржЖржЬржХрзЗрж░ рж╢рзЗржЦрж╛:

| ржмрж┐рж╖рзЯ | ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЦрзНржпрж╛ |
|------|----------|
| Table UI | ржбрзЗржЯрж╛ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржирзЛрж░ ржкрзНрж░ржлрзЗрж╢ржирж╛рж▓ рж╕рзНржЯрж╛ржЗрж▓

# ЁЯУИ Day 3: Dashboard Overview Cards with Tailwind CSS

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржорж╛ржжрзЗрж░ рж▓ржХрзНрж╖рзНржп:

```js
  },
```

## тЬЕ рзй. Dashboard Home Page тАУ Add Cards

ЁЯУД `pages/dashboard/index.js`

```jsx
import DashboardLayout from '@/components/DashboardLayout';
import stats from '@/data/stats';

export default function DashboardHome() {
  return (
    <DashboardLayout>
      <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">ЁЯУК Dashboard Overview</h2>

      {/* Stats Grid */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        {stats.map(stat => (
          <div key={stat.id} className={`rounded-xl p-6 shadow ${stat.color}`}>
            <div className="text-4xl">{stat.icon}</div>
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mt-2">{stat.title}</h3>
            <p className="text-3xl font-bold mt-1">{stat.value}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </DashboardLayout>
  );
}
```

---

## тЬЕ рзк. Tailwind Grid Explanation:

| ржХрзНрж▓рж╛рж╕ | ржХрж╛ржЬ |
|------|-----|
| `grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3` | responsive 1 тЖТ 2 тЖТ 3 columns  
| `rounded-xl p-6 shadow` | ржХрж╛рж░рзНржб рж╕рзНржЯрж╛ржЗрж▓  
| `${stat.color}` | ржбрж╛рзЯржирж╛ржорж┐ржХ рж░ржЩ ржпрзЛржЧ ржХрж░рж▓рж╛ржо  

---

## тЬЕ Output:

- тЬФя╕П 3ржЯрж┐ рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ рж░ржЩрж┐ржи ржХрж╛рж░рзНржб  
- тЬФя╕П ржорзЛржмрж╛ржЗрж▓/ржЯрзНржпрж╛ржм/ржбрзЗрж╕рзНржХржЯржкрзЗ responsive layout  
- тЬФя╕П ржкрзНрж░рждрж┐ ржХрж╛рж░рзНржбрзЗ Emoji/Icon + Title + рж╕ржВржЦрзНржпрж╛

---

## тЬЕ ржЖржЬржХрзЗрж░ рж╢рзЗржЦрж╛:

| ржЯржкрж┐ржХ | ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЦрзНржпрж╛ |
|------|----------|
| Stat Cards | Admin summary ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржирзЛрж░ UI  
| Tailwind Grid | responsive ржЧрзНрж░рж┐ржб  
| Dynamic Classes | ржПржХрж╛ржзрж┐ржХ ржХрж╛рж▓рж╛рж░ handle  
| Componentized Layout | ржХрж╛рж░рзНржб UI ржмрж╛рж░ржмрж╛рж░ ржмрзНржпржмрж╣рж╛рж░ ржХрж░рж╛ ржпрж╛ржмрзЗ

---

## ЁЯЫая╕П ржкрзНрж░рзНржпрж╛ржХржЯрж┐рж╕ ржХрж░рзЛ:

1. ржПржХржЯрж┐ ржирждрзБржи ржХрж╛рж░рзНржб ржпрзЛржЧ ржХрж░рзЛ тАУ ржпрзЗржоржи: тАЬPending ReviewsтАЭ

# ЁЯУ▒ Day 4: Sidebar UX тАУ Active Link Highlight + Mobile Toggle Menu

---

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржорж╛ржжрзЗрж░ ржЯрж╛рж░рзНржЧрзЗржЯ:

- Sidebar ржП ржХрзЛржи рж▓рж┐ржВржХрзЗ ржПржЦржи ржЖржЫрзЛ рж╕рзЗржЯрж╛ highlight рж╣ржмрзЗ  
- ржорзЛржмрж╛ржЗрж▓рзЗ toggle ржмрж╛ржЯржи ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ sidebar ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржирзЛ/рж▓рзБржХрж╛ржирзЛ ржпрж╛ржмрзЗ  
- рж╕ржм ржХрж┐ржЫрзБ responsive рж╣ржмрзЗ Tailwind ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ

---

## тЬЕ рзи. Use `useRouter()` to Get Current Page

ЁЯУД `components/DashboardLayout.js`

```jsx
import Link from 'next/link';
import { useRouter } from 'next/router';
import { useState } from 'react';

export default function DashboardLayout({ children }) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [menuOpen, setMenuOpen] = useState(false);

  const menuItems = [
    { name: "Dashboard", path: "/dashboard", icon: "ЁЯУК" },
    { name: "Users", path: "/dashboard/users", icon: "ЁЯСе" },
    { name: "Settings", path: "#", icon: "тЪЩя╕П" },
  ];

  return (
    <div className="flex h-screen bg-gray-100">
      {/* Sidebar */}
      <aside className={`${menuOpen ? 'block' : 'hidden'} md:block w-64 bg-white shadow-md p-4`}>
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">Admin Panel</h2>
        <ul className="space-y-3">
          {menuItems.map((item) => (
            <li key={item.path}>
              <Link
                href={item.path}
                className={`block px-4 py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-100 ${
                  router.pathname === item.path
                    ? 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 font-semibold'
                    : 'text-gray-700'
                }`}
              >
                {item.icon} {item.name}
              </Link>
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </aside>

      {/* Main Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col">
        {/* Topbar */}
        <header className="bg-white shadow p-4 flex justify-between items-center">
          <div className="md:hidden">
            <button
              onClick={() => setMenuOpen(!menuOpen)}
              className="text-gray-700 bg-gray-200 px-3 py-1 rounded"
            >
              тШ░ Menu
            </button>
          </div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold hidden md:block">Welcome Admin</h1>
          <button className="text-sm text-red-600">Logout</button>
        </header>

        {/* Page content */}
        <main className="p-6 overflow-y-auto">{children}</main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

---

## тЬЕ Output:

- тЬЕ Current page link bold & blue highlight  
- тЬЕ ржорзЛржмрж╛ржЗрж▓рзЗ тШ░ Menu ржмрж╛ржЯржирзЗ ржЯрж┐ржкрж▓рзЗ sidebar ржжрзЗржЦрж╛рзЯ  
- тЬЕ Desktop ржП рж╕ржмрж╕ржорзЯ sidebar ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ ржпрж╛рзЯ  
- тЬЕ Toggle ржмржирзНржз ржХрж░рж▓рзЗ sidebar ржЧрж╛рзЯрзЗржм рж╣рзЯ

---

## тЬЕ Tailwind Breakdown:

| ржХрзНрж▓рж╛рж╕ | ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЦрзНржпрж╛ |
|------|---------|
| `router.pathname` | Active route ржЪрзЗржХ ржХрж░рждрзЗ  
| `hidden md:block` | ржЫрзЛржЯ рж╕рзНржХрзНрж░рж┐ржирзЗ hide  
| `bg-blue-100 text-blue-700` | active рж╕рзНржЯрж╛ржЗрж▓  
| `setMenuOpen(!menuOpen)` | toggle sidebar state

---

## тЬЕ ржЖржЬржХрзЗрж░ рж╢рзЗржЦрж╛:

| ржЯржкрж┐ржХ | ржмрзНржпрж╛ржЦрзНржпрж╛ |
|------|----------|
| Active Link | route ржЪрзЗржХ ржХрж░рзЗ рж╣рж╛ржЗрж▓рж╛ржЗржЯ  
| Mobile Menu | toggle state ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ menu show/hide  
| Responsive Sidebar | ржЫрзЛржЯ рж╕рзНржХрзНрж░рж┐ржирзЗ menu ржХрж╛ржЬ ржХрж░рзЗ  
| Tailwind Utility | class conditionally handle ржХрж░рж╛

---

## ЁЯЫая╕П ржкрзНрж░рзНржпрж╛ржХржЯрж┐рж╕ ржХрж░рзЛ:

1. ржЖрж░рзЗржХржЯрж╛ page ржпрзЛржЧ ржХрж░рзЛ тАУ `/dashboard/settings.js`

ЁЯСЙ ржХрзЛржи Tailwind ржХрзНрж▓рж╛рж╕ ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ ржорзЛржмрж╛ржЗрж▓рзЗ рж▓рзБржХрж╛ржирзЛ ржпрж╛рзЯ?

# ЁЯЫая╕П Day 5: User Table Row Actions + Confirmation Modal

---

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржЬ ржЖржорж░рж╛ ржХрж░ржмрзЛ:

- ржкрзНрж░рждрж┐ ржЗржЙржЬрж╛рж░ row-рждрзЗ тАЬEditтАЭ ржУ тАЬDeleteтАЭ ржмрж╛ржЯржи  
- Delete ржЪрж╛ржкрж▓рзЗ ржПржХржЯрж┐ modal confirm ржХрж░ржмрзЗ  
- Edit ржПржЦржи placeholder рж░рж╛ржЦржмрзЛ (future-ready)

---

## тЬЕ рзи. Update `pages/dashboard/users.js`

### ЁЯФБ Update Table Row:

```jsx
<tbody className="text-gray-700 text-sm">
  {users.map((user) => (
    <tr key={user.id} className="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">
      <td className="py-3 px-6 font-medium">{user.name}</td>
      <td className="py-3 px-6">{user.email}</td>
      <td className="py-3 px-6">
        <span className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold
          ${user.role === "Admin" ? "bg-red-100 text-red-600" :
            user.role === "Editor" ? "bg-blue-100 text-blue-600" :
              "bg-gray-100 text-gray-600"}`}>
          {user.role}
        </span>
      </td>
      <td className="py-3 px-6">
        <button className="text-blue-600 hover:underline mr-3">Edit</button>
        <button
          onClick={() => handleDelete(user)}
          className="text-red-600 hover:underline"
        >
          Delete
        </button>
      </td>
    </tr>
  ))}
</tbody>
```

---

## тЬЕ рзй. Add Delete Modal (UI only)

```jsx
import { useState } from 'react';
import users from '@/data/users';
import DashboardLayout from '@/components/DashboardLayout';

export default function UsersPage() {
  const [showModal, setShowModal] = useState(false);
  const [selectedUser, setSelectedUser] = useState(null);

  const handleDelete = (user) => {
    setSelectedUser(user);
    setShowModal(true);
  };

  const closeModal = () => {
    setShowModal(false);
    setSelectedUser(null);
  };

  const confirmDelete = () => {
    console.log("Deleted:", selectedUser.name);
    closeModal();
  };

  return (
    <DashboardLayout>
      <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-6">ЁЯСе Users</h2>

      {/* Table... (from before) */}

      {/* Modal */}
      {showModal && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
          <div className="bg-white rounded-xl p-6 w-full max-w-sm text-center shadow-lg">
            <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4">Confirm Delete</h3>
            <p>Are you sure you want to delete <strong>{selectedUser.name}</strong>?</p>
            <div className="mt-6 flex justify-center gap-4">
              <button onClick={confirmDelete} className="bg-red-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded hover:bg-red-700">Yes, Delete</button>
              <button onClick={closeModal} className="bg-gray-200 px-4 py-2 rounded hover:bg-gray-300">Cancel</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </DashboardLayout>
  );
}
```

---

## тЬЕ Output:

- тЬЕ ржкрзНрж░рждрж┐ржЯрж┐ row-рждрзЗ Edit/Delete  
- тЬЕ Delete ржЪрж╛ржкрж▓рзЗ modal ржЦрзБрж▓рзЗ confirm ржЪрж╛рзЯ  
- тЬЕ тАЬYesтАЭ ржЪрж╛ржкрж▓рзЗ console log ржХрж░рзЗ  
- тЬЕ тАЬCancelтАЭ ржЪрж╛ржкрж▓рзЗ modal ржмржирзНржз рж╣рзЯ

## тЬЕ Tailwind Breakdown:

| ржХрзНрж▓рж╛рж╕ | ржХрж╛ржЬ |
|------|------|
| `fixed inset-0` | рж╕рзНржХрзНрж░рж┐ржиржЬрзБрзЬрзЗ overlay  
| `bg-opacity-50` | ржЕрж▓рзНржк ржХрж╛рж▓рзЛ ржмрзНржпрж╛ржХржЧрзНрж░рж╛ржЙржирзНржб  
| `z-50` | рж╕ржм ржХрж┐ржЫрзБрж░ ржЙржкрж░ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛рзЯ  
| `rounded-xl shadow` | рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ popup UI  
| `text-center`, `gap-4` | рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ layout ржУ alignment

1. Modal ржПрж░ ржнрж┐рждрж░рзЗ ржЗржЙржЬрж╛рж░рзЗрж░ рж░рзЛрж▓ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржУ

# ЁЯЫая╕П Day 1: Project Setup + MongoDB Connection + Note Schema

---

## тЬЕ рзз. Project Structure Overview

```
ЁЯУБ pages/
 тФЬтФАтФА index.js           тЖТ Homepage (Notes list)
 тФЬтФАтФА api/
 тФВ    тФФтФАтФА notes/
 тФВ        тФЬтФАтФА index.js   тЖТ GET/POST notes
 тФВ        тФФтФАтФА [id].js    тЖТ DELETE/PUT note by id
ЁЯУБ models/
 тФФтФАтФА Note.js             тЖТ Mongoose Schema
ЁЯУБ lib/
 тФФтФАтФА db.js               тЖТ MongoDB connection
ЁЯУБ components/
 тФФтФАтФА NoteCard.js         тЖТ Single note display
ЁЯУД .env.local             тЖТ MongoDB URI
```

---

## тЬЕ рзи. Step-by-Step Setup

---

### тЬЕ Step 1: Create Next.js Project

```bash
npx create-next-app@latest notes-app
cd notes-app
```

---

### тЬЕ Step 2: Install Packages

```bash
npm install mongoose
npm install -D tailwindcss postcss autoprefixer
npx tailwindcss init -p
```

---

### тЬЕ Step 3: Configure Tailwind

ЁЯУД `tailwind.config.js`

```js
content: [
  "./pages/**/*.{js,ts,jsx,tsx}",
  "./components/**/*.{js,ts,jsx,tsx}",
]
```

ЁЯУД `styles/globals.css`

```css
@tailwind base;
@tailwind components;
@tailwind utilities;
```

ЁЯУД `pages/_app.js`

```js
import '../styles/globals.css';

export default function App({ Component, pageProps }) {
  return <Component {...pageProps} />;
}
```

---

## тЬЕ рзй. MongoDB Setup

### тЬЕ Step 1: Create MongoDB Cluster  
ЁЯСЙ Go to [https://cloud.mongodb.com](https://cloud.mongodb.com)  
- Create free account  
- Create cluster  
- Whitelist IP: `0.0.0.0/0`  
- Create a user/password  
- Copy connection string

---

### тЬЕ Step 2: Add to `.env.local`

ЁЯУД `.env.local`

```
MONGODB_URI=mongodb+srv://username:password@cluster.mongodb.net/notes-app?retryWrites=true&w=majority
```

---

## тЬЕ рзк. Create MongoDB Connect File

ЁЯУД `lib/db.js`

```js
import mongoose from 'mongoose';

const connectDB = async () => {
  if (mongoose.connections[0].readyState) return;

  await mongoose.connect(process.env.MONGODB_URI, {
    useNewUrlParser: true,
    useUnifiedTopology: true
  });

  console.log("тЬЕ MongoDB Connected");
};

export default connectDB;
```

---

## тЬЕ рзл. Create Note Model

ЁЯУД `models/Note.js`

```js
import mongoose from 'mongoose';

const NoteSchema = new mongoose.Schema({
  title: {
    type: String,
    required: true,
  },
  content: {
    type: String,
    required: true,
  }
}, {
  timestamps: true
});

export default mongoose.models.Note || mongoose.model('Note', NoteSchema);
```

---

## тЬЕ Test: Console MongoDB Connect

ЁЯУД `pages/api/test.js`

```js
import connectDB from '@/lib/db';
import Note from '@/models/Note';

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  await connectDB();
  const test = await Note.find({});
  res.status(200).json({ success: true, notes: test });
}
```

тЮбя╕П Run server: `npm run dev`  
тЮбя╕П Visit: `http://localhost:3000/api/test` тЖТ тЬЕ MongoDB connected!

# ЁЯУй Day 2: Full CRUD API for Notes in Next.js (MongoDB)

---

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржорж╛ржжрзЗрж░ рж▓ржХрзНрж╖рзНржп:

- `GET` тЖТ рж╕ржм ржирзЛржЯ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ржУ  
- `POST` тЖТ ржирждрзБржи ржирзЛржЯ рждрзИрж░рж┐  
- `DELETE` тЖТ ржирж┐рж░рзНржжрж┐рж╖рзНржЯ ржирзЛржЯ ржорзБржЫрзЗ ржлрзЗрж▓рзЛ  
- `PUT` тЖТ ржирж┐рж░рзНржжрж┐рж╖рзНржЯ ржирзЛржЯ ржЖржкржбрзЗржЯ ржХрж░рзЛ

---

## тЬЕ рзи. API Routes Overview

ЁЯУБ `pages/api/notes/`  
```
тФЬтФАтФА index.js       тЖТ GET, POST (All notes, create note)
тФФтФАтФА [id].js        тЖТ GET, PUT, DELETE (Single note actions)
```

---

## тЬЕ рзй. `pages/api/notes/index.js`

```js
import connectDB from '@/lib/db';
import Note from '@/models/Note';

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  await connectDB();

  if (req.method === 'GET') {
    const notes = await Note.find({});
    return res.status(200).json({ notes });
  }

  if (req.method === 'POST') {
    const { title, content } = req.body;
    if (!title || !content) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Title and content required' });
    }

    const note = await Note.create({ title, content });
    return res.status(201).json({ note });
  }

  res.status(405).json({ error: 'Method not allowed' });
}
```

---

## тЬЕ рзк. `pages/api/notes/[id].js`

```js
import connectDB from '@/lib/db';
import Note from '@/models/Note';

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  await connectDB();
  const { id } = req.query;

  if (req.method === 'GET') {
    const note = await Note.findById(id);
    if (!note) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not found' });
    return res.status(200).json({ note });
  }

  if (req.method === 'PUT') {
    const { title, content } = req.body;
    const updated = await Note.findByIdAndUpdate(
      id,
      { title, content },
      { new: true }
    );
    return res.status(200).json({ updated });
  }

  if (req.method === 'DELETE') {
    await Note.findByIdAndDelete(id);
    return res.status(204).end();
  }

  res.status(405).json({ error: 'Method not allowed' });
}
```

---

## тЬЕ рзл. Test with Postman / Thunder Client (VS Code Extension)

**GET:**  
- `http://localhost:3000/api/notes`  
тЮбя╕П рж╕ржм ржирзЛржЯ ржжрзЗржЦрж╛ ржпрж╛ржмрзЗ

**POST:**  
- Body:
```json
{
  "title": "Test Note",
  "content": "This is a test note."
}
```

**DELETE:**  
- `http://localhost:3000/api/notes/<note-id>`

**PUT:**  
- Body:
```json
{
  "title": "Updated Title",
  "content": "Updated Content"
}
```

|-----|----------|
| API Route | Next.js ржПрж░ ржорж╛ржзрзНржпржорзЗ backend ржмрж╛ржирж╛ржирзЛ

# ЁЯУЭ Day 3: Note Form + Notes List (Frontend UI)

---

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржорж╛ржжрзЗрж░ рж▓ржХрзНрж╖рзНржп:

- Create Note form (`title`, `content`)  
- `POST /api/notes` ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ ржирждрзБржи note save  
- `GET /api/notes` ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ рж╕ржм note list  
- Tailwind ржжрж┐рзЯрзЗ рж╕рзБржирзНржжрж░ card UI

---

## тЬЕ рзи. NoteCard Component ржмрж╛ржирж╛ржУ

ЁЯУБ `components/NoteCard.js`

```jsx
export default function NoteCard({ note }) {
  return (
    <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded shadow hover:shadow-md transition">
      <h3 className="text-xl font-bold">{note.title}</h3>
      <p className="text-gray-600 mt-2">{note.content}</p>
    </div>
  );
}
```

---

## тЬЕ рзй. Homepage ржмрж╛ржирж╛ржУ: `pages/index.js`

```jsx
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import NoteCard from '@/components/NoteCard';

export default function Home() {
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState([]);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ title: '', content: '' });

  // Fetch notes on load
  useEffect(() => {
    fetchNotes();
  }, []);

  const fetchNotes = async () => {
    const res = await fetch('/api/notes');
    const data = await res.json();
    setNotes(data.notes);
  };

  const handleChange = (e) => {
    setForm({ ...form, [e.target.name]: e.target.value });
  };

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!form.title || !form.content) return alert("Fill all fields");

    const res = await fetch('/api/notes', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(form)
    });

    if (res.ok) {
      setForm({ title: '', content: '' });
      fetchNotes(); // Reload notes
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 py-10">
      <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-6">ЁЯЧТя╕П My Notes</h1>

      {/* Add Note Form */}
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4 mb-10 bg-white p-6 rounded shadow">
        <input
          name="title"
          placeholder="Note Title"
          value={form.title}
          onChange={handleChange}
          className="w-full border px-4 py-2 rounded"
        />
        <textarea
          name="content"
          placeholder="Note Content"
          value={form.content}
          onChange={handleChange}
          className="w-full border px-4 py-2 rounded"
        />
        <button
          type="submit"
          className="bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded hover:bg-blue-700"
        >
          тЮХ Add Note
        </button>
      </form>

      {/* Note List */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        {notes.map((note) => (
          <NoteCard key={note._id} note={note} />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

# тЬПя╕ПЁЯЧСя╕П Day 4: Edit & Delete Notes тАУ Modal UI + CRUD Integration

---

## тЬЕ рзз. ржЖржорж╛ржжрзЗрж░ рж▓ржХрзНрж╖рзНржп:

- ржкрзНрж░рждрж┐ржЯрж┐ ржирзЛржЯрзЗрж░ ржкрж╛рж╢рзЗ Edit ржУ Delete ржмрж╛ржЯржи  
- Edit ржЪрж╛ржкрж▓рзЗ modal form ржЦрзБрж▓ржмрзЗ  
- Update рж╣рж▓рзЗ ржирзЛржЯ рж░рж┐ржлрзНрж░рзЗрж╢ рж╣ржмрзЗ  
- Delete ржХрж░рж▓рзЗ confirm ржХрж░рзЗ remove ржХрж░ржмрзЗ

---

## тЬЕ рзи. Update `NoteCard.js` тАУ Add Buttons

ЁЯУД `components/NoteCard.js`

```jsx
export default function NoteCard({ note, onEdit, onDelete }) {
  return (
    <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded shadow hover:shadow-md transition">
      <h3 className="text-xl font-bold">{note.title}</h3>
      <p className="text-gray-600 mt-2">{note.content}</p>

      <div className="flex gap-4 mt-4 text-sm">
        <button
          onClick={() => onEdit(note)}
          className="text-blue-600 hover:underline"
        >
          тЬПя╕П Edit
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={() => onDelete(note._id)}
          className="text-red-600 hover:underline"
        >
          ЁЯЧСя╕П Delete
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

---

## тЬЕ рзй. Update `pages/index.js` тАУ Modal + Functions

```jsx
import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import NoteCard from "@/components/NoteCard";

export default function Home() {
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState([]);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ title: "", content: "" });
  const [editingNote, setEditingNote] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchNotes();
  }, []);

  const fetchNotes = async () => {
    const res = await fetch("/api/notes");
    const data = await res.json();
    setNotes(data.notes.reverse()); // latest first
  };

  const handleChange = (e) => {
    setForm({ ...form, [e.target.name]: e.target.value });
  };

  const handleEdit = (note) => {
    setEditingNote(note);
    setForm({ title: note.title, content: note.content });
  };

  const handleDelete = async (id) => {
    const confirm = window.confirm("Are you sure?");
    if (!confirm) return;

    await fetch(`/api/notes/${id}`, {
      method: "DELETE",
    });
    fetchNotes();
  };

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!form.title || !form.content) return;

    if (editingNote) {
      // UPDATE
      await fetch(`/api/notes/${editingNote._id}`, {
        method: "PUT",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(form),
      });
      setEditingNote(null);
    } else {
      // CREATE
      await fetch("/api/notes", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(form),
      });
    }

    setForm({ title: "", content: "" });
    fetchNotes();
  };

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 py-10">
      <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-6">ЁЯЧТя╕П My Notes</h1>

      {/* Form */}
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4 mb-10 bg-white p-6 rounded shadow">
        <input
          name="title"
          placeholder="Note Title"
          value={form.title}
          onChange={handleChange}
          className="w-full border px-4 py-2 rounded"
        />
        <textarea
          name="content"
          placeholder="Note Content"
          value={form.content}
          onChange={handleChange}
          className="w-full border px-4 py-2 rounded"
        />
        <button
          type="submit"
          className="bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded hover:bg-blue-700"
        >
          {editingNote ? "тЬПя╕П Update Note" : "тЮХ Add Note"}
        </button>
      </form>

      {/* Notes */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        {notes.map((note) => (
          <NoteCard
            key={note._id}
            note={note}
            onEdit={handleEdit}
            onDelete={handleDelete}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

- тЬЕ ржкрзНрж░рждрж┐ржЯрж┐ ржирзЛржЯрзЗрж░ ржкрж╛рж╢рзЗ Edit/Delete

---

### тЬЕ Step-by-step Deploy

1. ЁЯзСтАНЁЯТ╗ GitHub Repo ржмрж╛ржирж╛ржУ  
2. Terminal:
```bash
git init
git add .
git commit -m "Initial Commit"
git remote add origin https://github.com/yourname/notes-app.git
git push -u origin main
```

3. ЁЯМР Vercel ржП ржпрж╛ржУ тЖТ [https://vercel.com](https://vercel.com)  
4. тАЬ**New Project**тАЭ тЖТ GitHub ржерзЗржХрзЗ Import ржХрж░рзЛ  
5. `.env` variables ржмрж╕рж╛ржУ:
```
MONGODB_URI=your-full-mongo-uri
```

6. тЬЕ Deploy ржмрж╛ржЯржирзЗ ржХрзНрж▓рж┐ржХ ржХрж░рзЛ  
7. ЁЯОЙ Live link ржкрж╛ржмрзЗ: `https://notes-app.vercel.app`
